#	Format information:
#
#	Each line of this file consists of three tab-separated fields.
#
#	Field 0: the Tangut code point value in U+ format
#	Field 1: a tag indicating the type of information in the third field
#	Field 2: the value (in UTF-8)
#
#	Note that this tagged format is identical to that used
#	in the Unihan database files, so that it can be parsed
#	by the same tools.
#
#	Current tag list:
#
#	Tangut Merged source: kTGT_MergedSrc
#	Radical-Stroke indexes: kTGT_RSUnicode
#
# The following abbreviations are used in kTGT_MergedSrc:
